    /**
          * add a event track

         function addEventTrack(event, eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel) {
             dataLayer.push({
                 'event': event,
                 'eventCategory': eventCategory,
                 'eventAction': eventAction,
                 'eventLabel': eventLabel
             });
             return true;
         }
         //no small image
         function noSmallImage() {
             var img = event.srcElement;
             img.src = "//static.cdnsbg.com/public/images/default/sm/missing_image_thumb_de.jpg";
             img.onerror = null;
         }

      <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
       (function ($) {
             $.fn.hoverDelay = function (options) {
                 var defaults = {
                     hoverDuring: 100,
                     outDuring: 300,
                     hoverEvent: function () {
                         $.noop();
                     },
                     outEvent: function () {
                         $.noop();
                     }
                 };
                 var sets = $.extend(defaults, options || {});
                 var hoverTimer, outTimer, that = this;
                 return $(this).each(function () {
                     $(this).hover(function () {
                         clearTimeout(outTimer);
                         hoverTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                             sets.hoverEvent.apply(that)
                         }, sets.hoverDuring);
                     }, function () {
                         clearTimeout(hoverTimer);
                         outTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                             sets.outEvent.apply(that)
                         }, sets.outDuring);
                     });
                 });
             }
         })(jQuery);
         $(function () {
             try {
                 $(".newBut a").click(function () {
                     if ($("#back_phone").validate().form()) {
                         var opticianOption = '';
                         if ($("#opticianOption").is(":checked") == true) {
                             opticianOption = 'checked';
                         }
                         else {
                             opticianOption = 'none';
                         }
                         var email = $("input[name=email_address]").val();
                         $.ajax({
                             type: "POST",
                             url: "https://www.smartbuyglasses.de/help/send",
                             data: "comfirm_email=" + email + "&email_addr=" + email + "&frist_name=" + $("input[name=name]").val() + "&help_message=" + $("textarea[name=message]").val() + "&last_name=&location=HH" + "&order_id=" + $("input[name=orderid]").val() + "&phone=" + $("input[name=telephone]").val() + "&subject_select=Call me back" + "&verifyCode=back_call&opticianOption=" + opticianOption,
                             beforeSend: function () {
                                 $(".newBut").html('<img class="ajax_loader" src="//static.cdnsbg.com/en/images/ajax-loader.gif"/>');
                             },
                             success: function (response) {
                                 var jsonResponse = $.parseJSON(response);
                                 if (jsonResponse.success == 1) {
                                     $(".newBut").html("<div style='color:red;'>Ihre Nachricht wurde erfolgreich gesendet.</div>")
                                 }
                                 else {
                                     $(".newBut").html("<a href='#'>RÜCKRUF ERWÜNSCHT</a><div style='color:red;'>Ihre Nachricht konnte nicht gesendet werden. Bitte versuchen Sie es erneut.</div>")
                                 }
 
                             }
                         });
                     }
                     return false;
                 });
 
                 //promo day bar js
                 $(".promo_bar_big_close").click(function () {
                     $(".hp_topbigad_box").slideUp();
                     $(".hp_topsmallad_box").slideDown();
                     $("#header").addClass("small_top_dis").removeClass("big_top_dis");
                     $(".newtopBox").removeClass("mother_bigbanner_height").addClass("mother_smallbanner_height");
                 });
                 $(".promo_bar_to_big").click(function () {
                     $(".hp_topsmallad_box").slideUp();
                     $(".hp_topbigad_box").slideDown();
                     $(".newtopBox").removeClass("mother_smallbanner_height").addClass("mother_bigbanner_height");
                     $("#header").removeClass("small_top_dis").addClass("big_top_dis");
                 });
                 //close promo bar
                 $(".promo_bar_small_to_close").click(function () {
                     try {
                         $.post("/index/ajax-set-promo-bar-cookie/", {close_promo_bar: "yes"}, function (data) {
                         });
                         $(".hp_topsmallad_box").remove();
                         $(".hp_topbigad_box").remove();
                         $(".topbar_box").removeClass("mother_smallbanner_height");
                         $(".header_box").removeClass("small_top_dis");
                     } catch (e) {
                     }
                     $("#pro_infor_list").css("top", "99px");
                 });
             }
             catch (e) {
             }
 
             try {
                 jQuery.validator.addMethod("username", function (value, element) {
                     var userName = /[0-9&\|\\\*^%$#@!?,.`\~\/\[\]\-]/g;
                     return this.optional(element) || !userName.test(value);
                 });
                 jQuery.validator.addMethod("isPhone", function (value, element) {
                     var mobile = /^\d+$/;
                     var tel = /^[\+]?\d+-?\d+[\+]?$/;
                     return this.optional(element) || (tel.test(value) || mobile.test(value));
                 });
                 $("#back_phone").validate({
                     rules: {
                         name: {
                             required: true,
                             username: true
                         },
                         telephone: {
                             required: true,
                             isPhone: true
                         },
                         email_address: {
                             required: true,
                             email: true
                         },
                         message: {
                             required: true
                         }
                     },
                     messages: {
                         name: {
                             required: "Bitte geben Sie Ihren Namen ein",
                             username: "Bitte geben Sie Ihren richtigen Namen an"
                         },
                         telephone: {
                             required: "Bitte geben Sie Ihre Telefonnummer an",
                             isPhone: "Bitte geben Sie eine gültige Telefonnummer an"
                         },
                         email_address: {
                             required: "Bitte geben Sie Ihre E-Mail-Adresse ein",
                             email: "Bitte geben Sie Ihre richtige E-Mail-Adresse ein"
                         },
                         message: {
                             required: "Bitte geben Sie Ihre Nachricht ein"
                         }
                     },
                     highlight: function (element) {
                         $(element).closest('.control-group').removeClass('success').addClass('error');
                     },
                     success: function (element) {
                         element
                             .closest('.control-group').removeClass('error').addClass('success');
                     },
                     onfocusout: function (element) {
                         $(element).valid();
                     }
                 });
             }
             catch (e) {
             }
         });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       // js/slider/js/craftyslide.min.js
     (function($){$.fn.craftyslide=function(options){var defaults={"width":656,"height":324,"pagination":true,"fadetime":350,"delay":5000};var options=$.extend(defaults,options);return this.each(function(){var $this=$(this);var $slides=$this.find("ul.main_image").children("li");$slides.not(":first").hide();function paginate(){$this.append("<ol id='pagination' />");var i=1;$slides.each(function(){$(this).attr("id","slide"+i);$("#pagination").append("<li><a href='#slide"+i+"'>"+i+"</a></li>");i++});$("#pagination li a:first").addClass("active")}function captions(){$slides.each(function(){$caption=$(this).find("img").attr("title");if($caption!==undefined){$(this).prepend("<p class='caption'>"+$caption+"</p>")}$slides.filter(":first").find(".caption").css("bottom",0)})}function manual(){var $pagination=$("#pagination li a");$pagination.click(function(e){e.preventDefault();var $current=$(this.hash);if($current.is(":hidden")){$slides.fadeOut(options.fadetime);$current.fadeIn(options.fadetime);$pagination.removeClass("active");$(this).addClass("active");$(".caption").css("bottom","-37px");$current.find(".caption").delay(300).animate({bottom:0},300)}})}function auto(){setInterval(function(){var current_bigimg=$("#slideshow ul").find("li:visible");var next_bigimg=current_bigimg.next("li").eq(0);if(next_bigimg.attr("id")){current_bigimg.fadeOut(options.fadetime);next_bigimg.fadeIn(options.fadetime)}else{current_bigimg.fadeOut(options.fadetime);$("#slideshow ul li:first").fadeIn(options.fadetime)}$slides.each(function(){if($slides.is(":visible")){$(".caption").css("bottom","-37px");$(this).find(".caption").delay(300).animate({bottom:0},300)}});var current_active=$("#pagination li a.active");var next_a=current_active.parent("li").eq(0).next("li").eq(0).children("a").eq(0);if(next_a.attr("href")){next_a.addClass("active")}else{$("#pagination li:first a").addClass("active")}current_active.removeClass("active")},options.delay)}if($slides.length>1){if(options.pagination===true){paginate();auto()}else{paginate()}}captions();manual()})}})(jQuery);
 
     // index/image.js
     (function($){$.imageProperty=function(){var opts=$.imageProperty.defaults;var setProperty=new setProperty();function setProperty(){$("."+opts.indexBannerClass+" img").attr("width","656").attr("height","324");$("."+opts.rightBannerClass+" img").attr("width","280").attr("height","160");$("."+opts.brandImageClass+" img").attr("width","280").attr("height","160")}};$.imageProperty.defaults={indexBannerClass:"main_image",rightBannerClass:"index_small_pic",brandImageClass:"featured_deals"}})(jQuery);

      <script type="text/javascript">
       var referral_code_from_email = "";
         $(function () {
             //landing page from referral email
             if (referral_code_from_email != "" && referral_code_from_email != null && typeof(referral_code_from_email) != "undefined") {
                 $.post(webBaseUrl + "/referral/land", {referral_code: referral_code_from_email}, function (data) {
                     try {
                         var response = $.parseJSON(data);
                         if (response.status == "error") {
                             if (response.act == 'error-rfl001') {
                                 var warnAlert = "Sorry, aber der Rabattcode wurde bereits benutzt.";
                                 $.toolsFunction.showHintWin(warnAlert);
                             }
                         }
                     } catch (error) {
                         $.toolsFunction.showReferralPopup(data);
                     }
                 });
             }
             $("#hint_tips_win .hint_tips_close").live("click", function () {
                 $.toolsFunction.closeHintWin();
             });
             //product detail top
             $.imageProperty();
         });
      </script>
      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function () {
             $("#slideshow").craftyslide();
             function anim(duration) {
                 $('#mint').animate(
                     {height: 'toggle'},
                     {duration: duration, specialEasing: {height: 'easeOutBounce'}}
                 );
             }
 
             $('#closebtn').click(function () {
                 $('#mintbar').slideUp();
                 anim(800);
             });
 
             $('#mint').click(function () {
                 anim(500);
                 $('#mintbar').slideDown('slow', 'easeOutBounce');
             });
 
             $(".home_info ul li").live("mouseenter", function () {
                 $(this).addClass("selected_handly");
             }).live("mouseleave", function () {
                 $(this).removeClass("selected_handly");
             }).live("click", function () {
                 if ($(".caroufredsel_wrapper").hasClass("hide")) {
                     $(".main_text").addClass("hide");
                     $(".caroufredsel_wrapper").removeClass("hide");
                 }
                 $("#more_info").parent().removeClass("p_selected");
             });
 
             function page_title($c, $i) {
                 var title = $i.find("a img").attr('alt');
                 $('#title').text(title);
             }
 
             $(".seo_button a").click(function () {
                 $(".main_image").trigger("pause");
                 $(".caroufredsel_wrapper").css("display", "none");
                 $('.pageNum a').removeClass('selected');
                 $(this).addClass('selected');
             })
 
             $('.pageNum a').click(function () {
                 $(".main_image").trigger("resume");
                 $(".seo_button a").removeClass('selected');
                 $(".caroufredsel_wrapper").show();
                 $(this).addClass('selected');
                 var current = $(this).text();
                 $(".main_image").trigger("slideTo", current - 1);
             });
 
             $("#more_info").live("click", function () {
                 $(".main_text").removeClass("hide");
                 $(".caroufredsel_wrapper").addClass("hide");
                 $(this).parent().addClass("p_selected");
                 $("ul.home_nav li").each(function () {
                     $(this).removeClass("selected_handly").removeClass("selected");
                 });
                 return false;
             });
 
             $(".windowMask").click(function () {
                 remove_popup();
             });
 
             $(".eToolOverlay .luxottica_main_banners").mouseover(function () {
                 $(this).css("cursor", "pointer");
             });
 
             $(".index_small_pic ul>li:eq(0)").click(function () {
                 addEventTrack('GAEvent', 'Home banner', 'click', 'Discount Campaign Small Banner');
             });
 
             $("#Map2").click(function () {
                 addEventTrack('GAEvent', 'Home banner', 'click', 'Discount Campaign Modal Window links');
             });
         });
 
         function remove_popup1(div_obj, windowMask) {
             $(div_obj).fadeOut('normal');
             $('div' + windowMask).fadeOut('normal');
         }
 
         function return_popup1(div_obj, top, left, windowMask) {
             var zoomPopTop = getPopTop1(top);
             var zoomPopLeft = getPopLeft1(left);
 
             addMask1(windowMask);
             $(div_obj).fadeIn('normal');
             $(div_obj).css('top', zoomPopTop + 'px');
             $(div_obj).css('left', zoomPopLeft + 'px');
         }
 
         function getPopTop1(top) {
             var scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop + document.body.scrollTop;
             var windowHeight = window.outerHeight;
             if ($.browser.msie) {
                 windowHeight = window.screen.availHeight;
             }
             var popTop = (windowHeight - top) / 2 + scrollTop;
             return popTop;
         }
 
         function getPopLeft1(left) {
             var scrollLeft = document.documentElement.scrollLeft + document.body.scrollLeft;
             var windowWidth = window.outerWidth;
             if ($.browser.msie) {
                 windowWidth = window.screen.availWidth;
             }
             var popLeft = (windowWidth - left) / 2 + scrollLeft;
             var formatPopLeft = windowWidth - left;
             return formatPopLeft;
         }
 
         function addMask1(windowMask) {
             var windowMask = $('div' + windowMask);
             windowMask.fadeIn('normal');
             windowMask.css('height', $('body').height());
             windowMask.css('width', $('body').width());
         }
 
         function getNewVerify() {
             var timestamp = Math.round(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
             $('#verifyImg').attr('src', '/help/print-verify-img' + "?" + timestamp);
         }
      </script>
      <script src="https://static.cdnsbg.com/en/js/showbox/dialog.js?v=1530691074" type="text/javascript">
      </script>

       $(function () {
                         $("#popOK").click(function () {
                 remove_popup1("#myOnPageContent", ".windowMask");
             });
         });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function(event){
         $('img.lazy').lazyload({effect:'fadeIn'});
         try{
             $('.pro_slider_sun img.lazy').each(function(){var _this = $(this);_this.attr('src',_this.attr('data-original'))});
             var sliderSun = new TouchSlider('pro_slider_sunglasses', {duration: 800, interval: 3000,direction: 0, autoplay: false, align: 'left', mousewheel: false, mouse: true, fullsize: false, visibleCount: 4});
             $('.pro_slider_sun .prev').click(function(){sliderSun.prev(4);});
             $('.pro_slider_sun .next').click(function(){sliderSun.next(4);});
         }catch(e){console.error('slide sun error.', e);}
 
         try{
             $('.pro_slider_eye img.lazy').each(function(){var _this = $(this);_this.attr('src',_this.attr('data-original'))});
             var sliderEye = new TouchSlider('pro_slider_eyeglasses', {duration: 800, interval: 3000,direction: 0, autoplay: false, align: 'left', mousewheel: false, mouse: true, fullsize: false, visibleCount: 4});
             $('.pro_slider_eye .prev').click(function(){sliderEye.prev(4);});
             $('.pro_slider_eye .next').click(function(){sliderEye.next(4);});
         }catch(e){console.error('slide eye error', e);}
 
         try {
             var slideEl = $("#home-banner-slide li")
             var homeBanerSlide=new TouchSlider('home-banner-slide',{
                 duration:600,			//int 页面过渡时间
                 direction:0,			//int 页面切换方向，0横向，1纵向
                 start:0,				//int 默认显示页面
                 align:'center',			//string 对齐方式，left(top) center(middle) right(bottom)
                 mouse:true,				//bool 是否启用鼠标拖拽
                 mousewheel:false,		//bool 是否启用鼠标滚轮切换
                 arrowkey:false,			//bool 是否启用键盘方向切换
                 fullsize:true,			//bool 是否全屏幻灯（false为自由尺寸幻灯）
                 autoplay:true,	    	//bool 是否自动播放幻灯
                 interval:4000			//bool 幻灯播放时间间隔
             });
             slideEl.hover(function () {
                 homeBanerSlide.pause();
             }, function () {
                 homeBanerSlide.play();
             });
             console=window.console || {dir:new Function(),log:new Function()};
             var active=0,
                 as=$('#pagenavi .pagevi-num li');
             for(var i=0;i<as.length;i++){
                 (function(){
                     var j=i;
                     as[i].onclick=function(){
                         homeBanerSlide.slide(j);
                         return false;
                     }
                 })();
             }
             homeBanerSlide.on('before',function(m,n){
                 as[m].className='';
                 as[n].className='active';
             });
         } catch (e) {
             console.error('Home banners slide error', e);
         }
 
                     });
      </script>

                     });

                 sbgGrcWidget = grecaptcha.render('sbg-g-recaptcha', {
                     'sitekey': '6Le9IhsTAAAAAJAlfO4qoozgtIvPa1FF_CMILylL',
                 });
             };

    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
     (function($){
 	/**
 	 * this is a plugin for favorite product
 	 * @author Alan shen & John
 	 */
 	//****fav's collection function****//
     $.myFavsHeart = function(options) {
         var options = $.extend({},
         {
             favProductsAddUrl: "/fav-products/add-favs/",
             favProductsRemoveUrl: "/fav-products/remove-favs/",
             actionAdd: "add",
             actionRemove: "remove",
             favsHeartClassName: "fav_heart_tag",
             favsimgDir: "/",
             favoriteTipsAdd: "Add to Favorites",
             favoriteTipsRemove: "Remove from Favorites",
             favStatusClassSelect: "click",
             favStatusClassRemove: "remove_icon",
             favsTipsClassName: "fav_iconP",
             ajax_error: "servers error",
             headerFavsClassName: "favorCount",
             topFavRemoveName: "topFavRemove",
             topFavListUiId: "favorite_display",
             favsAdditionTotalPriceTextId: "favs_total_price_text",
             showFavCounts: 4,
             favsAdditionalText: "",
             favsAdditionalTexts: "",
             additionCountText: "addition_count_text",
             favoriteEmptyDivId: "favorite_empty",
             favoriteFullDivId: "favorite_full",
             favoriteDisplayDivId: "favoriteDisplayDiv",
             favoriteDisplay: "favoriteDisplay",
             favHideTotalPriceId: "favHideTotalPrice",
             noShowTipsName: "no_show_tips",
             HeartFavTip: "Favorites",
             Controller: "default",
             QickView:"A"
         },
         options);
         var favsMain = new favsMain();
         function favsMain() {
             var fav_heart_tag = $("." + options.favsHeartClassName + ",." + options.topFavRemoveName);
             var fav_heart_tag_mouse = $("." + options.favsHeartClassName);
             var favsAdditionTotalPrice = 0;
             var showItemPrice = 0;
             var recProInfo = $(".recProInfo,.recProInf");
             var favHideTotalPrice = $("#" + options.favHideTotalPriceId).val();
             if (favsAdditionTotalPrice == 0) {
                 favsAdditionTotalPrice = parseFloat(favHideTotalPrice)
             }
             fav_heart_tag_click();
             var ifMouseOver = false;
             fav_heart_tag_mouse.live("mouseover",
             function() {
                 var itemsClassSplit = $(this).attr("class").split(" ");
                 if (!inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itemsClassSplit)) {
                     if (inItems(options.favStatusClassSelect, itemsClassSplit)) {
                         $(this).removeClass(options.favStatusClassSelect).addClass(options.favStatusClassRemove);
                         addFavsTips($(this), options.favoriteTipsRemove)
                     } else {
                         addFavsTips($(this), options.favoriteTipsAdd)
                     }
                 }
             });
             fav_heart_tag_mouse.live("mouseout",
             function() {
                 ifMouseOver = false;
                 var itemsClassSplit = $(this).attr("class").split(" ");
                 if (!inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itemsClassSplit)) {
                     removeFavTips($(this));
                     if (inItems(options.favStatusClassRemove, itemsClassSplit)) {
                         $(this).removeClass(options.favStatusClassRemove).addClass(options.favStatusClassSelect)
                     }
                 }
             });
             $("#" + options.favoriteDisplayDivId).hoverDelay({
                 hoverEvent: function() {
                     checkShowWhichFav();
                     $(this).addClass("hoverli");
                     $(this).find("#" + options.favoriteDisplay).addClass("addblock")
                 },
                 outEvent: function() {
                     checkShowWhichFav();
                     $(this).find("#" + options.favoriteDisplay).removeClass("addblock")
                 }
             });
             recProInfo.live("mouseover",
             function() {
                 var fav_icon = $(this).find(".fav_icon");
                 if (fav_icon.length > 0) {
                     recProInfoMouseOver($(this))
                 }
             });
             recProInfo.live("mouseout",
             function() {
                 var fav_icon = $(this).find(".fav_icon");
                 if (fav_icon.length > 0) {
                     recProInfoMouseOut($(this))
                 }
             });
             function recProInfoMouseOver(recProInfo) {
                 if(options.QickView == 'A')
                 {
                 	var moreInfo = recProInfo.children(".morecolor").eq(0);
                     if (moreInfo.length > 0) {
                         moreInfo.hide()
                     }
                 }
                 try{
                 recProInfo.find(".pro_view_quick").eq(0).show();
                 recProInfo.find(".pro_quick_view").eq(0).show();
 				recProInfo.find(".pro_vq_bg").eq(0).show();
 				}catch(e){}
 				
                 recProInfo.find(".fav_icon").eq(0).show();
                 ceateHeartFavTip(options.HeartFavTip, recProInfo)
             }
             function recProInfoMouseOut(recProInfo) {
             	if(options.QickView == 'A')
                 {
                     var moreInfo = recProInfo.children(".morecolor").eq(0);
                     if (moreInfo.length > 0){
                         moreInfo.show()
                     }
                 }
                 try{
                 recProInfo.find(".pro_view_quick").eq(0).hide();
                 recProInfo.find(".pro_quick_view").eq(0).hide();
 				recProInfo.find(".pro_vq_bg").eq(0).hide();
 			    }catch(e){}
                 var fav_icon_div = recProInfo.find(".fav_icon");
                 var itemsClassSplit = fav_icon_div.children(".fav_iconI").eq(0).attr("class").split(" ");
                 if (!inItems(options.favStatusClassSelect, itemsClassSplit)) {
                     fav_icon_div.eq(0).hide()
                 }
                 removeHeartFavTip(recProInfo)
             }
             function showHeartSingle(recProInfo) {
                 recProInfo.find(".fav_icon").eq(0).show()
             }
             function hideHeartSingle(recProInfo) {
                 var fav_icon_div = recProInfo.find(".fav_icon");
                 var itemsClassSplit = fav_icon_div.children(".fav_iconI").eq(0).attr("class").split(" ");
                 if (!inItems(options.favStatusClassSelect, itemsClassSplit)) {
                     fav_icon_div.eq(0).hide()
                 }
             }
             function fav_heart_tag_click(obj) {
                 if (obj == null || obj == "") {
                     obj = fav_heart_tag
                 }
                 if (options.Controller == "new-glasses" || options.Controller == "contact-lenses") {
                     obj.on("click",
                     function() {
                         var mySelf = $(this);
                         mySelf.unbind(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                         fav_heart_tag_func_click(mySelf)
                     });
                     $("." + options.topFavRemoveName).unbind("click").on("click",
                     function() {
                         var mySelf = $(this);
                         mySelf.unbind(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                         fav_heart_tag_func_click(mySelf)
                     })
                 } else {
                     obj.live("click",
                     function() {
                         var mySelf = $(this);
                         mySelf.unbind(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                         fav_heart_tag_func_click(mySelf)
                     })
                 }
             }
             function fav_heart_tag_func_click(obj) {
                 ifMouseOver = true;
                 var act = obj.attr("action");
                 var categoryId = obj.attr("cateid");
                 var pid = obj.attr("pid");
                 var mySelf = obj;
                 if (act == options.actionAdd) {
                     var addTagItem = $("." + options.favsHeartClassName + "[cateid='" + categoryId + "']" + "[pid='" + pid + "']");
                     addTagItem.addClass(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                     obj.addClass(options.favStatusClassRemove);
                     var itClassSplit = obj.attr("class").split(" ");
                     if (!inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itClassSplit)) {
                         removeFavTips(obj)
                     }
                     addTagItem.attr("action", options.actionRemove);
                     if (ifMouseOver) {
                         if (!inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itClassSplit)) {
                             addFavsTips(obj, options.favoriteTipsRemove)
                         }
                     }
                     addTagItem.each(function() {
                         var recProInfo = $(this).parents(".recProInfo").eq(0);
                         if (recProInfo.length <= 0) {
                             var recProInfo = $(this).parents(".recProInf").eq(0)
                         }
                         if (recProInfo.length > 0) {
                             showHeartSingle(recProInfo)
                         }
                     });
                     $.ajax({
                         type: "POST",
                         url: options.favProductsAddUrl + "categoryId/" + categoryId + "/pid/" + pid,
                         beforeSend: function() {},
                         success: function(response) {
                             var jsonResponse = $.parseJSON(response);
                             var products = jsonResponse.product;
                             if (jsonResponse.status == "success") {
                                 dealCurrentFavsCount(options.actionAdd);
                                 addFavoriteData(products)
                             } else {
                                 var itemsClassSplit = obj.attr("class").split(" ");
                                 if (inItems(options.favStatusClassSelect, itemsClassSplit)) {
                                     addTagItem.removeClass(options.favStatusClassSelect)
                                 }
                                 if (inItems(options.favStatusClassRemove, itemsClassSplit)) {
                                     addTagItem.removeClass(options.favStatusClassRemove)
                                 }
                                 addTagItem.attr("action", options.actionAdd)
                             }
                             fav_heart_tag_click(obj);
                             if (inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itClassSplit)) {
                                 var favoriteEmptyDivId = options.favoriteEmptyDivId;
                                 var favoriteFullDivId = options.favoriteFullDivId;
                                 $("#" + favoriteEmptyDivId).hide();
                                 $("#" + favoriteFullDivId).show()
                             }
                         }
                     })
                 } else {
                     if (act == options.actionRemove) {
                         var isTopFavRemove = false;
                         var itemsClassSplit = obj.attr("class").split(" ");
                         if (inItems(options.topFavRemoveName, itemsClassSplit)) {
                             isTopFavRemove = true
                         }
                         var removeTagItem = $("." + options.favsHeartClassName + "[cateid='" + categoryId + "']" + "[pid='" + pid + "']");
                         try {
                             if (typeof(removeTagItem) != "undefined") {
                                 var itemsClassSplitTop = removeTagItem.attr("class").split(" ");
                                 removeTagItem.removeClass(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                                 removeTagItem.removeClass(options.favStatusClassRemove);
                                 if (!isTopFavRemove) {
                                     removeFavTips(obj);
                                     if (ifMouseOver) {
                                         if (!inItems(options.noShowTipsName, itemsClassSplit)) {
                                             addFavsTips(obj, options.favoriteTipsAdd)
                                         }
                                     }
                                     removeTagItem.attr("action", options.actionAdd)
                                 } else {
                                     removeTagItem.attr("action", options.actionAdd)
                                 }
                             }
                         } catch(e) {}
                         removeTagItem.each(function() {
                             var recProInfo = $(this).parents(".recProInfo").eq(0);
                             if (recProInfo.length <= 0) {
                                 var recProInfo = $(this).parents(".recProInf").eq(0)
                             }
                             if (recProInfo.length > 0) {
                                 hideHeartSingle(recProInfo)
                             }
                         });
                         $.ajax({
                             type: "POST",
                             url: options.favProductsRemoveUrl + "categoryId/" + categoryId + "/pid/" + pid,
                             beforeSend: function() {},
                             success: function(response) {
                                 var jsonResponse = $.parseJSON(response);
                                 if (jsonResponse.status == "success") {
                                     dealCurrentFavsCount(options.actionRemove);
                                     if (isTopFavRemove) {
                                         var price = 0
                                     } else {
                                         var price = parseFloat(jsonResponse.price)
                                     }
                                     removeTopItemData(pid, categoryId, price)
                                 } else {
                                     removeTagItem.addClass(options.favStatusClassSelect);
                                     removeTagItem.attr("action", options.actionRemove)
                                 }
                                 fav_heart_tag_click(obj)
                             }
                         })
                     }
                 }
             }
             function addFavoriteData(json) {
                 if (json != null) {
                     if (json.length > 0) {
                         htmlString = "";
                         $.each(json,
                         function(key, v) {
                             var styleDisHtml = "";
                             var favsCount = getFavsCount();
                             var showFavCounts = parseInt(options.showFavCounts);
                             var formatPri = $.toolsFunction.formatPrice(v.selling_price);
                             if (favsCount > showFavCounts) {
                                 styleDisHtml = ' style="display:none" '
                             }
                             htmlString += "<li itemprice=" + v.selling_price + ' id="fav_top_item_' + v.category_id + "_" + v.product_id + '"';
                             htmlString += styleDisHtml + ">";
                             htmlString += '<div class="cartlist">';
                             htmlString += '<div class="product_img">';
                             htmlString += '<a href="' + v.product_link + '"><img src="' + v.image + '" width="104px"></a>';
                             htmlString += "</div>";
                             htmlString += '<div class="product_con">';
                             htmlString += '<p><a href="' + v.product_link + '">' + v.product_name + "</a></p>";
                             htmlString += "</div>";
                             htmlString += '<div class="product_pri">';
                             htmlString += "<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" action='remove' cateid='" + v.category_id + "' pid='" + v.product_id + '\' class="closeIcon topFavRemove">';
                             htmlString += '<i class="fa fa-times-circle"></i>';
                             htmlString += "</a>";
                             htmlString += '<span><a href="' + v.product_link + '">' + formatPri + "</a></span>";
                             htmlString += "</div>";
                             htmlString += '<div class="clear"></div>';
                             htmlString += "</div>";
                             htmlString += "</li>";
                             if (favsCount > showFavCounts) {
                                 favsAdditionTotalPrice = parseFloat(favsAdditionTotalPrice) + parseFloat(v.selling_price);
                                 favsAdditionTotalPrice = favsAdditionTotalPrice.toFixed(2);
                                 var favsAdditionTotalPriceText = $.toolsFunction.formatPrice(favsAdditionTotalPrice);
                                 $("#" + options.favsAdditionTotalPriceTextId).text(favsAdditionTotalPriceText);
                                 var additionalNum = favsCount - showFavCounts;
                                 var displayAdditionTextHtml = formatFavsAdditionalText(additionalNum);
                                 $("#" + options.additionCountText).text(displayAdditionTextHtml);
                                 $("#" + options.favsAdditionTotalPriceTextId).parent("p").show()
                             }
                             favsCount++
                         });
                         $("#" + options.topFavListUiId).append(htmlString)
                     }
                 }
                 return true
             }
             function removeTopItemData(pid, cateid, price) {
                 var favsCount = getFavsCount();
                 var showFavCounts = parseInt(options.showFavCounts);
                 var noShowFlag = false;
                 if ($("#fav_top_item_" + cateid + "_" + pid).css("display") == "none") {
                     noShowFlag = true
                 }
                 $("#fav_top_item_" + cateid + "_" + pid).remove();
                 if (favsCount <= 0) {
                     var favoriteEmptyDivId = options.favoriteEmptyDivId;
                     var favoriteFullDivId = options.favoriteFullDivId;
                     $("#" + favoriteEmptyDivId).show();
                     $("#" + favoriteFullDivId).hide()
                 }
                 if (favsCount <= showFavCounts) {
                     $("#" + options.favsAdditionTotalPriceTextId).parent("p").hide()
                 }
                 if (favsCount >= showFavCounts) {
                     if (noShowFlag == false) {
                         showFirstHideItem()
                     }
                     if (favsCount > showFavCounts) {
                         if (price == 0) {
                             var removePrice = showItemPrice;
                             showItemPrice = 0
                         } else {
                             var removePrice = price
                         }
                         favsAdditionTotalPrice = parseFloat(favsAdditionTotalPrice) - parseFloat(removePrice);
                         favsAdditionTotalPrice = favsAdditionTotalPrice.toFixed(2)
                     } else {
                         favsAdditionTotalPrice = 0
                     }
                     var favsAdditionTotalPriceText = $.toolsFunction.formatPrice(favsAdditionTotalPrice);
                     $("#" + options.favsAdditionTotalPriceTextId).text(favsAdditionTotalPriceText);
                     var additionalNum = favsCount - showFavCounts;
                     var displayAdditionTextHtml = formatFavsAdditionalText(additionalNum);
                     $("#" + options.additionCountText).text(displayAdditionTextHtml)
                 }
                 return true
             }
             function checkShowWhichFav() {
                 var favsCount = getFavsCount();
                 if (favsCount > 0) {
                     $("#" + options.favoriteEmptyDivId).hide();
                     $("#" + options.favoriteFullDivId).show()
                 } else {
                     $("#" + options.favoriteEmptyDivId).show();
                     $("#" + options.favoriteFullDivId).hide()
                 }
             }
             function showFirstHideItem() {
                 var items = $("#" + options.topFavListUiId + " li");
                 if (items != null) {
                     $.each(items,
                     function(k, v) {
                         if ($(this).css("display") == "none") {
                             $(this).show();
                             showItemPrice = $(this).attr("itemprice");
                             return false
                         }
                     })
                 }
                 return true
             }
             function objToJson(obj) {
                 var jsonStr = JSON.stringify(obj);
                 return (jsonStr != "" && jsonStr != null) ? jsonStr: ""
             }
             function jsonToObj(json) {
                 var obj = $.parseJSON(json);
                 return obj != null ? obj: null
             }
             function dealCurrentFavsCount(act) {
                 var favsCount = getFavsCount();
                 if (act == options.actionAdd) {
                     favsCount = favsCount + 1
                 } else {
                     if (act == options.actionRemove && favsCount > 0) {
                         favsCount = favsCount - 1
                     }
                 }
                 $("#" + options.headerFavsClassName).text(favsCount)
             }
             function getFavsCount() {
                 var favsCount = parseInt($("#" + options.headerFavsClassName).text());
                 return favsCount
             }
             function formatFavsAdditionalText(additionalNum) {
                 if (additionalNum > 1 && additionalNum != null) {
                     var displayAdditionTextHtml = options.favsAdditionalTexts.replace(/\d+/g, additionalNum)
                 } else {
                     var displayAdditionTextHtml = options.favsAdditionalText.replace(/\d+/g, additionalNum)
                 }
                 return displayAdditionTextHtml
             }
             function addFavsTips(obj, tipStr) {
                 var favsTipsAddHtml = createFavsTipsHtml(tipStr);
                 obj.append(favsTipsAddHtml);
                 showFavTips(obj);
                 return true
             }
             function removeFavTips(obj) {
                 obj.children("." + options.favsTipsClassName).remove();
                 return true
             }
             function showFavTips(obj) {
                 obj.children("." + options.favsTipsClassName).show();
                 return true
             }
             function createFavsTipsHtml(tipString) {
             	if(options.QickView == 'A'){
             	    var favsT = "<div class='" + options.favsTipsClassName + "'><p class='favs_tips'>" + tipString + "</p><img src='" + options.favsimgDir + "/preArrow6.png' alt='arrow'/></div>";
                 }
             	else{
             		var favsT = "";
                 }
                 return favsT;
             }
             function ceateHeartFavTip(tipString, target) {
                 if (target.children(".my_favsT").length > 0) {
                     target.children(".my_favsT").eq(0).show();
                 } else {
                     if(options.QickView == 'A')
                     {
                     	var favsT = '<li class="my_favsT">' + tipString + "</li>";
                         target.append(favsT);
                     }
                 }
                 return true
             }
             function removeHeartFavTip(target) {
                 target.children(".my_favsT").eq(0).hide();
                 return true
             }
             function inItems(needle, arr) {
                 if (typeof(arr) != "undefined") {
                     var l = parseInt(arr.length);
                     var i = 0;
                     if (l > 0) {
                         for (; i < l; i++) {
                             if (needle == arr[i]) {
                                 return true
                             }
                         }
                     }
                 }
                 return false
             }
         }
     };
